
2021-07-08

# Chief Complaint
- Blurred Vision
- Muscle Tenderness
- Tingling in Hands and Feet
- Thirst
- Confusion
- Sleep Disturbances
- Decreased Visual Perception


# History of Present Illness
Cherilyn
 is a 85 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of acute viral pharyngitis (disorder), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), viral sinusitis (disorder), suspected covid-19, fracture of ankle, severe anxiety (panic) (finding, covid-19, fever (finding), limited social contact (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), cough (finding), loss of taste (finding), social isolation (finding), stress (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
warfarin sodium 5 mg oral tablet; verapamil hydrochloride 40 mg; simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; milnacipran hydrochloride 100 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; digoxin 0.125 mg oral tablet; duloxetine 20 mg delayed release oral capsule; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]; naproxen sodium 220 mg oral tablet

# Assessment and Plan
Patient is presenting with social isolation (finding). 

## Plan

- assessment of anxiety (procedure)
- assessment using morse fall scale (procedure)

- assessment using alcohol use disorders identification test - consumption (procedure)

- Muscle Tenderness
- Tingling in Hands and Feet
- Thirst
- Confusion
- Sleep Disturbances
- Decreased Visual Perception


# History of Present Illness
Cherilyn
 is a 84 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of acute viral pharyngitis (disorder), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), viral sinusitis (disorder), suspected covid-19, fracture of ankle, severe anxiety (panic) (finding, covid-19, fever (finding), limited social contact (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), cough (finding), loss of taste (finding), social isolation (finding), stress (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
warfarin sodium 5 mg oral tablet; verapamil hydrochloride 40 mg; simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; milnacipran hydrochloride 100 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; digoxin 0.125 mg oral tablet; duloxetine 20 mg delayed release oral capsule; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]; naproxen sodium 220 mg oral tablet

# Assessment and Plan
Patient is presenting with stress (finding). 

## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- electrical cardioversion
- assessment of health and social care needs (procedure)
- medication reconciliation (procedure)
- assessment of anxiety (procedure)
- assessment using morse fall scale (procedure)
- depression screening (procedure)
- depression screening using patient health questionnaire two-item score (procedure)
- assessment of substance use (procedure)
- screening for drug abuse (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- verapamil hydrochloride 40 mg
- digoxin 0.125 mg oral tablet
- amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet
- warfarin sodium 5 mg oral tablet

- Tingling in Hands and Feet
- Thirst
- Confusion
- Sleep Disturbances
- Decreased Visual Perception


# History of Present Illness
Cherilyn
 is a 80 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of limited social contact (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), viral sinusitis (disorder), social isolation (finding), stress (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

- Muscle Tenderness
- Tingling in Hands and Feet
- Thirst
- Confusion
- Sleep Disturbances
- Decreased Visual Perception


# History of Present Illness
Cherilyn
 is a 75 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of limited social contact (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), social isolation (finding), stress (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Medicare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- assessment of health and social care needs (procedure)
- assessment using morse fall scale (procedure)
- screening for domestic abuse (procedure)
- depression screening (procedure)
- depression screening using patient health questionnaire two-item score (procedure)
- assessment of substance use (procedure)
- assessment using alcohol use disorders identification test - consumption (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet

2000-03-30

# Chief Complaint
- Blurred Vision
- Muscle Tenderness
- Tingling in Hands and Feet
- Thirst
- Confusion
- Sleep Disturbances
- Decreased Visual Perception


# History of Present Illness
Cherilyn
 is a 64 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of victim of intimate partner abuse (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Blue Cross Blue Shield.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

 is a 58 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of victim of intimate partner abuse (finding).

 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

 is a 52 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of victim of intimate partner abuse (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has UnitedHealthcare.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet

 is a 48 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of victim of intimate partner abuse (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Anthem.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet

 is a 43 year-old non-hispanic white female. Patient has a history of victim of intimate partner abuse (finding).

# Social History
Patient is single. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has a high school education.
Patient currently has Aetna.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- amlodipine 2.5 mg oral tablet
